| | | | | |     Dev16 (#3)
| | | | | |     
| | | | | |     fixes of deployment scripts, formatting. Added some requires of specific versions of libraries.  separate init_configs.sh script.
| | | | | |     
| | | | | |     docker_scripts/lib/_run.py: I dont know if the problem with with libtmux or tmux itself, but things were generally breaking when there were multiple processess (!) or when there were multiple threads, not even talking to the tmux socket at the same time i think, just subsequently. So, the logtail logic is now merged into _run.py, so there is only one process, and there is one thread with a loop doing the comms.
| | | | | |     Also we now use tmux even for non-parallel builds.

*   commit 1966e3c1
|\  Merge: 57a924c0 59c148a0
| | Author: koo5 <kolman.jindrich@gmail.com>
| | Date:   Thu Jun 8 11:00:43 2023 +0200
| | 
| |     Merge pull request #147 from lodgeit-labs/dev15
| |     
| |     Dev15
| |     
| |     simplified docs and dev deployment scripts / streamlined the cli parameters
| |     
| |     worker container is now deployed in two replicas by default (pretty arbitrary, just testing..)
| |     each worker container runs two processess, one only consuming the "health" queue. This way, health checks should always process quickly, and long jobs should queue up.
| |     up.py is the "ultimate" runner script that deploys the stack and starts retrying a request until timeout or success. When the script suceed, it can be said the stack is up and ready to accept requests. This could have been handled by docker health checks, but not really. At the least, it's not clear how to healtcheck a workqueue worker without potentially confusing things by also involving a broker, which would then bite us in larger scale/swarm deployments.
| |     
| |     corrected parallelization in frontend server.
| |     Started on an option to submit .xlsx files.
| |

| | 
| |     Merge branch 'dev9'
| |     
| |     Much evolved docker deployment script. One outstanding issue is that it still has to be installed, rather than ran in-place. Another may be that the tmux logic is rather ugly, and it would be best if *everything*
| |     Celery+flower was replaced with remoulade+dramatiq. Celery was too complicated, with many toggles to wiggle to make it work as was needed, and wannabe smart stack magic that made debugging impossible.
| |     lots of reorg/cleanups.
| |     improved python dependency handling
| |     django replaced with fastapi (for frontend and services). Django was not a good fit, we're not building an orm web app, no need to have route declarations spread across three different files, etc.
| |     just a couple of changes in prolog code.
| |     a beginning of a new test runner in /tests2.

| | 
| |     Prolog Server code restructured.
| |     
| |     Prolog server is restructured for consistency. All requests come to the prolog server. Server then calls the appropriate processing operation. Loan and Ledger directories process the loan and ledger requests respectively.
| |     
| |     Some noticable changes are:
| |     - ledger-request.xml file is modified. It now refers to a schema. <accountHierarchyUrl> node is removed (loading account hierarchy from local server).  A sample ledger-request is added in the ledger folder.
| |     - taxonomy folder added to store taxonomy related files.
| |     - loan-response is updated to XBRL instance. A sample response is added in the loan folder.

| Date:   Mon Apr 16 00:56:02 2018 -0500
| 
|     fix: recompute incr_and_sum key list with callable
|     
|     Change the `WindowRateLimiter` to pass a callable to `incr_and_sum` so
|     that during atomic increments the time windows can be recomputed in the
|     event of a lock.
|     
|     This breaks the API because we change `incr_and_sum`'s `keys` arg to
|     a callable. We keep backwards compatibility by checking if `keys` is
|     callable and calling it on each use.
|
